! Description: DomainVoider focuses on: Active Phishing hosts, both UTF-8 & ASCII domains, licensed to us by Hardenize.com;
! Malicious, exploited hosts including general malware & crypto jacking. Tracking domains & adserver domains are blocked, as are mainstream social sites.
! Orignally created for AdGuard Pro, DomainVoider function with both uBlock Origin & AdGuard for FireFox.
! When used with these extensions, the included $CSP rules help to strenghten the security of the entire web.
